     <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
      function showHideLiteB ()
 	{
 		b = document.getElementById ( 'basket' );
 		src = '';
 		if ( b.style.display == '' )
 		{
 			b.style.display = 'none';
 			src = '/images/ui/basket_images/Basket-1_r9_c3.jpg';
 		}
 		else
 		{
 			b.style.display = '';
 			src = '/images/ui/basket_images/Basket-1_r9_c3_flip.jpg';
 		}
 		
 		im = document.getElementById ( "shhide_img" );
 		im.src = src;
 	}
     </script>

        function onstch(se, id)
 			{
 				return;
 				i_ug_1 = document.getElementById('i_ug_1');
 				i_ug_2 = document.getElementById('i_ug_2');
 				
 				i_us_1 = document.getElementById('i_us_1');
 				i_us_2 = document.getElementById('i_us_2');
 				
 				switch ( se )
 				{
 					case 1:
 						document.getElementById('search_bar_id_site').style.display = 'none';
 						document.getElementById('search_bar_id_google').style.display = '';
 						document.getElementById('q').value = document.getElementById('q_id').value;
 						
 						i_us_1.style.borderColor = '#FFF';
 						i_us_2.style.borderColor = '#FFF';
 						
 						i_ug_1.style.borderColor = '#F90';
 						i_ug_2.style.borderColor = '#F90';
 						
 						break;
 					case 2:
 						document.getElementById('search_bar_id_google').style.display = 'none';
 						document.getElementById('search_bar_id_site').style.display = '';
 						document.getElementById('q_id').value = document.getElementById('q').value;
 						
 						i_us_1.style.borderColor = '#F90';
 						i_us_2.style.borderColor = '#F90';
 						
 						i_ug_1.style.borderColor = '#FFF';
 						i_ug_2.style.borderColor = '#FFF';
 						
 						break;
 				}
 			}
       </script>
